***снятие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тие</a> (10400)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снять.html>снять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">snjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">snjátije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>taking off, removal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крест.html>креста́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">snjátije s krestá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">deposition</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:покрытие.html>покры́тия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>snjátije</b> pokrýtija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stripping/removal of a coating</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>withdrawal, removal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́нег</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:счет.html>счёта</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>snjátije</b> déneg so sčóta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">withdrawal of money from a bank account; drawing on a bank account</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:эксплуатация.html>эксплуата́ции</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>snjátije</b> s ekspluatácii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">withdrawal/removal from service</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учет.html>учёта</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>snjátije</b> s učóta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">removal from the register</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>snjátije</b> s rabóty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dismissal, removal from office</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>gathering, harvest, reaping</li>
<li>ending
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:запрещение.html>запреще́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>snjátije</b> zapreščénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">removal/lifting of a ban</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:взыскание.html>взыска́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>snjátije</b> vzyskánija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">remission of punishment</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:осада.html>оса́ды</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>snjátije</b> osády</i> ― <span class="e-translation">raising of a siege</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:секретность.html>секре́тности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>snjátije</b> sekrétnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">declassification, disclosure</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>in expressions</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:копия.html>ко́пий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">snjátije kópij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">copying, duplication</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снятие.html>сня́тие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:показание.html>показа́ний</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">snjátije pokazánij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reading, readout</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***снять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:снять.html>снять</a> (561)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъnęti</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъ(n)-</i> (see <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъ(n)</i>) + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ęti</i>. Reanalyzed as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from which other words in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> were created, such as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нанять.html>наня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nanjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обнять.html>обня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снять.html>снять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">snjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снимать.html>снима́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take off, to take away, to take down</li>
<li>to take, to make</li>
<li>to photograph, to film</li>
<li>to rent <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">e.g. an apartment</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***со.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> (86)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">so</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>with <i>(+ instrumental case)</i></li>
<li>off, from <i>(+ genitive case)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This is a variant of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> before words beginning with certain awkward consonant clusters such as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мн-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mn-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вс-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vs-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сн-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sn-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>Предло́г</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>предло́га</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> буквосочетаниями <b>сн</b>, <b>рт</b>, <b>вс</b>, <b>мн</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> т. п. <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

***собака.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a> (467)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iranian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Iranian languages">Middle Iranian</a></span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zoroastrian_Dari_language" class="extiw" title="w:Zoroastrian Dari language">Zoroastrian Dari</a></span> <small>[script needed]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xme-ker-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sabah</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Median_language" class="extiw" title="w:Median language">Old Median</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="xme-old">σπάκα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xme-old-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spā́kəʰ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> [the source of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">ասպակ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aspak</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dog</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>], <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avestan" class="extiw" title="w:Avestan">Avestan</a></span> <i class="Avst mention" lang="ae">𐬯𐬞𐬀𐬐𐬀</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ae-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spaka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dog-like</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobáka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">саба́ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sabáka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">sobaka</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sobáka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dog
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пёс</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pjos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторожевой.html>сторожева́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">storoževája <b>sobáka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">watchdog</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дворовый.html>дворо́вая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dvoróvaja <b>sobáka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">cur, mongrel, mutt</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зарытый.html>зары́та</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vot gde <b>sobáka</b> zaryta!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Now I see it!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jevó káždaja <b>sobáka</b> znájet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Everyone knows him.</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">Every dog knows him</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голодный.html>голо́дный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">golódnyj kak <b>sobáka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">as hungry as a dog; wolfish, rapacious</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замерзнуть.html>замёрзнуть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zamjórznutʹ kak <b>sobáka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be chilled to the marrow</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>злой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zloj kak sobáka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mad as hell</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ке</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятый.html>пя́тая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">núžnyj kak <b>sobáke</b> pjátaja nogá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">need like a hole in the head</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сено.html>се́не</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sobáka na séne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dog in the manger</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:съесть.html>съесть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sobáku sʺjestʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to know something inside out</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устать.html>уста́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ustátʹ kak sobáka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be dog-tired</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>hound
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">соба́ка-ище́йка</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sobáka-iščéjka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">bloodhound</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobáka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собачий.html>соба́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sobáčij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dog; dog's, canine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:собачий.html>соба́чий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>хо́лод</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sobáčij</b> xólod</i> ― <span class="e-translation">beastly cold</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>dog's</b> cold</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собачник.html>соба́чник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sobáčnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собачник.html>соба́чника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собачник.html>соба́чники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собачник.html>соба́чников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">соба́чница</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:собеседование.html>собесе́дование</a> (17603)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собеседование.html>собесе́дование</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sobesédovanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собеседование.html>собесе́дования</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собеседование.html>собесе́дования</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собеседование.html>собесе́дований</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>interview <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a formal meeting for the assessment of a candidate or applicant</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> talk
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говориться.html>говори́тся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молитва.html>моли́тва</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:собеседование.html>собесе́дование</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:живой.html>живо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́гом</a>.</i><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | ru 1 | </a></sup><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Částo govorítsja, što molítva — éto <b>sobesédovanije</b> méždu živój dušój i Bógom.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It is often said that a prayer is a talk between a living soul and God.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собирать.html>собира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***собирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:собирать.html>собира́ть</a> (1316)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-birátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собирать.html>собира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sobirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собрать.html>собра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to gather, to collect, to harvest</li>
<li>to assemble</li>
<li>to convoke</li>
<li><i>(for a journey)</i> to equip, to prepare</li>
<li>(<i>programming</i>) to build, to compile</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собирать.html>собира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собираться.html>собира́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sobirátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собраться.html>собра́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to gather</li>
<li>to assemble</li>
<li>to be about to</li>
<li>to be going to, to intend, to mean</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собирать.html>собира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соблазнительный.html>соблазни́тельный</a> (11208)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соблазнить.html>соблазни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soblaznítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соблазнительный.html>соблазни́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soblaznítelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>seductive</li>
<li>alluring, enticing</li>
<li>provocative</li>
<li>tempting</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соблазн.html>собла́зн</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">soblázn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
